+Int128 Int128Mul(long64 lhs, long64 rhs) {

+inline double DistanceSqrd(const IntPoint& pt1, const IntPoint& pt2) {

+double DistanceFromLineSqrd(const IntPoint& pt, const IntPoint& ln1, const IntPoint& ln2) {
src/third_party/gdstk/external/clipper/clipper.cpp:3814: trailing whitespace.
+    // The equation of a line in general form (Ax + By + C = 0)
src/third_party/gdstk/external/clipper/clipper.cpp:3815: trailing whitespace.
+    // given 2 points (xą,yą) & (x˛,y˛) is ...
src/third_party/gdstk/external/clipper/clipper.cpp:3816: trailing whitespace.
+    //(yą - y˛)x + (x˛ - xą)y + (y˛ - yą)xą - (x˛ - xą)yą = 0

src/third_party/gdstk/external/clipper/clipper.cpp:3818: trailing whitespace.

+    double B = double(ln2.X - ln1.X);

+    double C = A * ln1.X + B * ln1.Y;

+    C = A * pt.X + B * pt.Y - C;

+    return (C * C) / (A * A + B * B);
